Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 116 (the Apollo 12 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Ron Burkey, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 116 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-071
	19:09 AUG. 11,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

021118,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021119,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021120,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 116.
021121,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
021122,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 12.
021123,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
021124,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
021125,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
021126,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
021127,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 494-616
021128,000012:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
021129,000013:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021130,000014:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021131,000015:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2017-01-22 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.
021132,000016:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-28 RSB  WTIH -> WITH.
021133,000017:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-09 HG   Transcribed
021134,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-13 RSB  Proofed comment text via 3-way diff vs
021135,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              Luminary 99 and 131.
021136,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-16 RSB  Comment-text fixes identified in 5-way
021137,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              side-by-side diff of Luminary 69/99/116/131/210.
021138,000022:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-19 HG   Fix operator CALL  --> VLOAD
021139,000023:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix statement CA BIT1  --> CS BIT5
021140,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand   ENDRRD29 --> ENDR29RD

021145,000029:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021146,000030:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021147,000031:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021148,000032:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021149,000033:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021150,000034: 
021151,000035:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021152,000036:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
021153,000037:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021154,000038:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021155,000039:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021156,000040: 
021157,000041:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021158,000042:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021159,000043:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
021160,000044:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
021161,000045:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
021162,000046:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
021163,000047:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021164,000048:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021165,000049:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
021166,000050:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
021167,000051:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
021168,000052:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021169,000053:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021170,000054:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021171,000055:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021172,000056:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021173,000057:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021174,000058:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021175,000059:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021176,000060:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021177,000061:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021178,000062:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
021179,000063:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021180,000064:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
021181,000065: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021182,000066: 
021183,000067: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021184,000068: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021185,000069: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021186,000070: 
021187,000071: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021188,000072: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021189,000073: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20

021617,000501:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021618,000502:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021619,000503:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
021620,000504:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021621,000505:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021622,000506: 
021623,000507:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021624,000508:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021625,000509:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021626,000510:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021627,000511:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021628,000512:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021629,000513:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021630,000514:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
021631,000515:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
021632,000516:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
021633,000517:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
021634,000518:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
021635,000519:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021636,000520:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021637,000521:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021638,000522:                                                                                                  #    NONE
021639,000523:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021640,000524:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

021643,000527:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

021689,000573:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021690,000574:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021691,000575:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021692,000576:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
021693,000577:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021694,000578: 
021695,000579:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021696,000580:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021697,000581:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021698,000582:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
021699,000583:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
021700,000584:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021701,000585:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
021702,000586:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
021703,000587:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
021704,000588:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021705,000589:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021706,000590:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021707,000591:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021708,000592:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021709,000593:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
021710,000594:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021711,000595:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021712,000596:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
021713,000597:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021714,000598:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
021715,000599:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021716,000600:                                                                                                  #    NOANGFLG
021717,000601:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021718,000602:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3

021895,000779:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021896,000780:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021897,000781:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021898,000782:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
021899,000783:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021900,000784: 
021901,000785:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021902,000786:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021903,000787:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021904,000788:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
021905,000789:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
021906,000790:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021907,000791:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021908,000792:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021909,000793:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021910,000794:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021911,000795:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021912,000796:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021913,000797:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021914,000798:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021915,000799:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021916,000800:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021917,000801:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
021918,000802:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021919,000803:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
021920,000804:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021921,000805:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021922,000806:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021923,000807:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
021924,000808:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021925,000809:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
021926,000810: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021927,000811: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021928,000812: 24,2675           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021929,000813: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND

022100,000984:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM

022104,000988:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022105,000989: 
022106,000990:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022107,000991:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -

022112,000996:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022113,000997:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022114,000998:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23

022171,001055:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022172,001056:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022173,001057:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022174,001058:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022175,001059:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022176,001060: 
022177,001061:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022178,001062:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022179,001063:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022180,001064:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022181,001065:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
022182,001066:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
022183,001067:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
022184,001068:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
022185,001069:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022186,001070:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
022187,001071:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
022188,001072:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
022189,001073:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022190,001074:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
022191,001075:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022192,001076:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022193,001077:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022194,001078:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022195,001079:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022196,001080:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022197,001081:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022198,001082:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022199,001083:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022200,001084:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
022201,001085: 24,3207  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022202,001086: 24,3207                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022203,001087: 24,3207           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022204,001088: 24,3210           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022205,001089: 24,3211           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022206,001090: 24,3212           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022207,001091: 24,3213           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO

022273,001157:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022274,001158:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022275,001159:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO : 3                      DATE: 4-11-67
022276,001160:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY : P VOLANTE  SDC
022277,001161: 
022278,001162: 
022279,001163:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
022280,001164:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
022281,001165:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
022282,001166:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.
022283,001167:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE-
022284,001168:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022285,001169:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R61LEM
022286,001170:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022287,001171:                                                                                                  #      LPS20.1       VECPOINT
022288,001172:                                                                                                  #      KALCMAN3
022289,001173: 
022290,001174: 
022291,001175:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022292,001176:                                                                                                  #    NORMAL RETURN IS TO CALLER + 1
022293,001177:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022294,001178:                                                                                                  #    TERMINATE P20 + R61 BY BRANCHING TO P20END IF BOTH TRACKFLAG +
022295,001179:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.
022296,001180:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022297,001181:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FOR LPS20.1 + ATTITUDE MANEUVER ROUTINE (R60)
022298,001182:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022299,001183:                                                                                                  #    GENRET USED TO SAVE Q FOR RETURN
022300,001184:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022301,001185:                                                                                                  #    3AXISFLG
022302,001186:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022303,001187:                                                                                                  #    SEE SUBROUTINES
022304,001188: 23,2000                                           SETLOC   R61                                   
022305,001189: 23,2000                                           BANK

022309,001193: 23,2117           55142                           TS       GENRET

022487,001371:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022488,001372: 
022489,001373:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022490,001374:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022491,001375:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022492,001376:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
022493,001377:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022494,001378:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022495,001379:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022496,001380:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022497,001381:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022498,001382:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022499,001383:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022500,001384:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
022501,001385:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022502,001386:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022503,001387:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
022504,001388: 
022505,001389:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022506,001390:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022507,001391:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022508,001392: 
022509,001393:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022510,001394:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022511,001395:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022512,001396:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
022513,001397: 
022514,001398:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
022515,001399: 
022516,001400:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022517,001401: 
022518,001402:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022519,001403: 
022520,001404:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022521,001405:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022522,001406:

022567,001451:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
022568,001452: 
022569,001453:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022570,001454:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022571,001455:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022572,001456:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022573,001457:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022574,001458:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022575,001459:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022576,001460:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022577,001461:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
022578,001462:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022579,001463:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022580,001464:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022581,001465:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022582,001466:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022583,001467:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022584,001468:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022585,001469:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022586,001470:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022587,001471:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022588,001472:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
022589,001473:

022591,001475:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF
022592,001476: 
022593,001477:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022594,001478:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022595,001479: 
022596,001480:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022597,001481: 
022598,001482:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

022638,001522:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022639,001523: 
022640,001524:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022641,001525: 
022642,001526:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022643,001527:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022644,001528:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022645,001529:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022646,001530:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022647,001531:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022648,001532:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022649,001533:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
022650,001534:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022651,001535:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022652,001536:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022653,001537:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
022654,001538: 
022655,001539:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022656,001540:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
022657,001541:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022658,001542: 
022659,001543:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022660,001544:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
022661,001545: 
022662,001546:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022663,001547: 
022664,001548:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022665,001549:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022666,001550: 
022667,001551:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022668,001552: 
022669,001553:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_   TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022670,001554: 
022671,001555: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022672,001556: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022673,001557: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022674,001558: 
022675,001559: 25,2073  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

022686,001570:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022687,001571: 
022688,001572:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022689,001573:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022690,001574:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022691,001575:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022692,001576:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022693,001577:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
022694,001578:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022695,001579:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022696,001580:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
022697,001581:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
022698,001582:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022699,001583:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022700,001584:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022701,001585:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022702,001586:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022703,001587:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022704,001588: 
022705,001589:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022706,001590:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022707,001591:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022708,001592: 
022709,001593:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022710,001594: 
022711,001595:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022712,001596:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022713,001597: 
022714,001598:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022715,001599: 
022716,001600:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022717,001601: 
022718,001602: 25,2102           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
022719,001603: 25,2103           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
022720,001604: 25,2104           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
022721,001605: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022722,001606: 25,2106           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
022723,001607: 25,2107           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
022724,001608: 25,2110           00002                           DEC      2          B-14

022760,001644:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022761,001645:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022762,001646:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022763,001647:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022764,001648:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022765,001649:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022766,001650:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
022767,001651:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022768,001652:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
022769,001653:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022770,001654:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022771,001655:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022772,001656:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022773,001657:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
022774,001658:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022775,001659:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022776,001660:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022777,001661:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022778,001662:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
022779,001663:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022780,001664:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
022781,001665:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022782,001666:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022783,001667:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
022784,001668: 
022785,001669:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022786,001670:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022787,001671:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022788,001672: 
022789,001673:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022790,001674:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
022791,001675: 
022792,001676:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022793,001677:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022794,001678: 
022795,001679:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022796,001680:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022797,001681: 
022798,001682:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022799,001683: 
022800,001684:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022801,001685: 
022802,001686: 25,2140           02167        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022803,001687:

022849,001733:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022850,001734: 
022851,001735:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022852,001736:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
022853,001737:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022854,001738:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022855,001739:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022856,001740:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022857,001741:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022858,001742:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022859,001743:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022860,001744:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022861,001745:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022862,001746:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022863,001747:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
022864,001748:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022865,001749:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022866,001750:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
022867,001751:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022868,001752:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022869,001753:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
022870,001754:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022871,001755: 
022872,001756:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022873,001757:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022874,001758:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022875,001759:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022876,001760:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
022877,001761: 
022878,001762:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022879,001763:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
022880,001764: 
022881,001765:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022882,001766:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022883,001767:

022885,001769:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022886,001770:

022943,001827:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022944,001828: 
022945,001829:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022946,001830:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022947,001831:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
022948,001832:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022949,001833:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
022950,001834:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
022951,001835:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022952,001836:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022953,001837:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
022954,001838:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022955,001839:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
022956,001840:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022957,001841:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022958,001842:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022959,001843:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
022960,001844: 
022961,001845:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE*  (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022962,001846:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
022963,001847:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
022964,001848:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022965,001849:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022966,001850: 
022967,001851:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022968,001852:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022969,001853:

022971,001855:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
022972,001856:

022974,001858:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022975,001859:

023031,001915:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM

023033,001917:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023034,001918:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023035,001919:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023036,001920:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023037,001921:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023038,001922:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023039,001923:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023040,001924:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
023041,001925:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023042,001926:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023043,001927:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023044,001928:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023045,001929:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023046,001930:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023047,001931: 
023048,001932:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023049,001933:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023050,001934:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023136,002020:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023137,002021: 
023138,002022:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023139,002023:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023140,002024:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023141,002025:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023142,002026:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023143,002027:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023144,002028:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023145,002029:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023146,002030:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023147,002031:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023148,002032:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023149,002033:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023150,002034:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023151,002035:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023152,002036:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023153,002037:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023154,002038:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023155,002039:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023156,002040:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023157,002041:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023158,002042:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023159,002043:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023160,002044:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023161,002045: 
023162,002046:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023163,002047:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023164,002048:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
023165,002049:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023166,002050:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023167,002051: 
023168,002052:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023169,002053:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
023170,002054: 
023171,002055:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023172,002056:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023173,002057:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
023174,002058:

023176,002060:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023177,002061:
