023223,002107:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023224,002108: 
023225,002109:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023226,002110:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023227,002111:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023228,002112:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023229,002113:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023230,002114:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023231,002115:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023232,002116:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023233,002117:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023234,002118:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
023235,002119:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023236,002120:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
023237,002121:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023238,002122:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023239,002123:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023240,002124:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023241,002125:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023242,002126:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023243,002127:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023244,002128:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023245,002129:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023246,002130: 
023247,002131:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023248,002132:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023249,002133: 
023250,002134:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023251,002135:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023252,002136: 
023253,002137:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023254,002138:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR, WAITLIST
023255,002139: 
023256,002140:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_

023395,002279:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023396,002280: 
023397,002281:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023398,002282:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023399,002283:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023400,002284:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
023401,002285:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023402,002286:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023403,002287:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
023404,002288:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023405,002289:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
023406,002290:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023407,002291:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023408,002292:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023409,002293:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023410,002294:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023411,002295:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023412,002296:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023413,002297:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
023414,002298:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023415,002299:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023416,002300:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023417,002301:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023418,002302:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023419,002303:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
023420,002304:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023421,002305:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023422,002306:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023423,002307: 
023424,002308:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023425,002309:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023426,002310:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023427,002311:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023428,002312: 
023429,002313:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023430,002314:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023431,002315: 
023432,002316:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023433,002317:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023434,002318: 
023435,002319:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023436,002320: 
023437,002321:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023438,002322:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023439,002323: 
023440,002324:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023441,002325:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023442,002326:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023443,002327: 
023444,002328: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES                              
023445,002329:

023487,002371:

Page 549 

023489,002373:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023490,002374: 
023491,002375:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023492,002376:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023493,002377:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023494,002378:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023495,002379:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
023496,002380:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023497,002381:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
023498,002382:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
023499,002383:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023500,002384:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE
023501,002385:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023502,002386:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023503,002387:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE
023504,002388:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023505,002389:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023506,002390:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023507,002391:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023508,002392:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
023509,002393:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023510,002394:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023511,002395:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023512,002396:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023513,002397:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023514,002398:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023515,002399:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023516,002400:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023517,002401:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023518,002402:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023519,002403:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023520,002404:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023521,002405:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023522,002406:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
023523,002407:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023524,002408:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023525,002409:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023526,002410:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023527,002411:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023528,002412:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
023529,002413: 
023530,002414:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023531,002415:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023532,002416: 
023533,002417:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023534,002418:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023535,002419:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023536,002420: 
023537,002421:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023538,002422:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
023539,002423:

Page 550 

023541,002425: 
023542,002426:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023543,002427:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023544,002428: 
023545,002429:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023546,002430: 
023547,002431:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023548,002432: 
023549,002433: 25,2646           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023550,002434: 25,2647           30036                           DCA      CDUT                                  
023551,002435: 25,2650           53107                           DXCH     TANG

023554,002438: 
023555,002439: 25,2652           77201                           SETPD    VLOAD                                 
023556,002440: 25,2653           00001                                    0

023604,002488:                                                                                                  #           AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE. CONVERT THIS TO A
023605,002489:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

023612,002496: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
023613,002497: 25,2733           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT
023614,002498: 25,2734           12737                           BZF      +3                                    #  GYRO CAUSES A POSITIVE CHANGE IN THE
023615,002499: 25,2735           31107                           CA       TANG       +1                         #  SHAFT ANGLE. COMPENSATE FOR THIS SWITCH

024219,003103:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024220,003104:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.  2      BY  J.D. COYNE    SDC    DATE 12-7-66
024221,003105: 
024222,003106:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024223,003107:                                                                                                  #  1) EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
024224,003108:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
024225,003109:                                                                                                  #  3) COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
024226,003110: 
024227,003111: 
024228,003112:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE       CALL
024229,003113:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
024230,003114: 
024231,003115: 
024232,003116:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024233,003117: 
024234,003118:                                                                                                  #  LEMPREC,CSMPREC
024235,003119: 
024236,003120:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_ RETURN TO CALLER + 2
024237,003121: 
024238,003122: 
024239,003123:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_ NONE
024240,003124: 
024241,003125: 
024242,003126:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_ NONE
024243,003127: 
024244,003128:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
024245,003129: 
024246,003130:                                                                                                  #  LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
024247,003131:                                                                                                  #  MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV

024372,003256:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024373,003257:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
024374,003258: 
024375,003259: 
024376,003260:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024377,003261: 
024378,003262:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
024379,003263:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
024380,003264:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024381,003265: 
024382,003266:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024383,003267: 
024384,003268: 
024385,003269:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024386,003270: 
024387,003271: 
024388,003272:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024389,003273: 
024390,003274:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
024391,003275:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
024392,003276:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
024393,003277:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
024394,003278:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024395,003279: 
024396,003280: 
024397,003281:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024398,003282: 
024399,003283:                                                                                                  #                00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024400,003284:                                                                                                  #                00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024401,003285: 
024402,003286: 
024403,003287:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024404,003288:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024405,003289: 
024406,003290:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024407,003291:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024408,003292: 
024409,003293:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024410,003294: 
024411,003295:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024412,003296:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
024413,003297:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
024414,003298:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
024415,003299:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
024416,003300: 
024417,003301: 
024418,003302:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024419,003303: 
024420,003304:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:
024421,003305:

Page 573

024425,003309:

024564,003448: 
024565,003449:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
024566,003450:                                                                                                  #     2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS
024567,003451: 
024568,003452: 
024569,003453:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE- BANKCALL FOR LRS22.2
024570,003454: 
024571,003455: 
024572,003456:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED: G+N,AUTO   SETMAXDB
024573,003457:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT - RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO +0 (VIA SWRETURN)
024574,003458:

024577,003461:

024580,003464: 
024581,003465:

024583,003467:                                                                                                  #       RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR-A HALF UNIT VECTOR COMPUTED BY LRS22.1
024584,003468:                                                                                                  #       RM - RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024585,003469:                                                                                                  #       BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 -INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE

Page 578 

024620,003504:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024621,003505:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
024622,003506:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024623,003507: 
024624,003508:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024625,003509: 
024626,003510:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024627,003511:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024628,003512:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024629,003513: 
024630,003514:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024631,003515:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024632,003516:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
024633,003517:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
024634,003518:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024635,003519:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024636,003520:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024637,003521: 
024638,003522: 
024639,003523:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024640,003524:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
024641,003525:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
024642,003526: 
024643,003527:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024644,003528:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024645,003529:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024646,003530:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024647,003531:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024648,003532:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
024649,003533: 
024650,003534: 
024651,003535:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024652,003536:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024653,003537:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
024654,003538:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024655,003539:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024656,003540:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024657,003541:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
024658,003542:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024659,003543:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
024660,003544:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
024661,003545:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
024662,003546:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
024663,003547:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
024664,003548:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
024665,003549:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
024666,003550: 
024667,003551:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024668,003552:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
024669,003553:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)
024670,003554:

Page 579 

024672,003556:                                                                                                  #   ULC,RXZ,SINTHETA,LGRET,RDRET,BVECTOR,W.IND,X78T
024673,003557: 
024674,003558: 
024675,003559: 13,2207                                           BANK     13

025069,003953:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025070,003954:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025071,003955:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025072,003956:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025073,003957: 
025074,003958:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025075,003959:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
025076,003960:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
025077,003961: 
025078,003962:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025079,003963:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025080,003964:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025081,003965:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025082,003966:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025083,003967:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025084,003968:

Page 587 

025086,003970:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

025088,003972:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025089,003973:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025090,003974:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025091,003975:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025092,003976:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG

025233,004117: 
025234,004118:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY
025235,004119:                                                                                                  #  RXZ = (SQRT (1-SINTHETA**2))RLC
025236,004120:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025237,004121:                                                                                                  #   ULC IN ULC, PD0
025238,004122:                                                                                                  #   RLC IN PD36D
025239,004123:                                                                                                  #   SIN THETA IN SINTHETA AND PD6
025240,004124:                                                                                                  #   RXZ NORM IN RXZ (N IN X1)

025293,004177: 
025294,004178:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025295,004179:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE   SDC         DATE 1-15-67
025296,004180: 
025297,004181: 
025298,004182:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025299,004183: 
025300,004184:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025301,004185:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025302,004186:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025303,004187:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025304,004188: 
025305,004189: 
025306,004190:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025307,004191: 
025308,004192: 
025309,004193:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025310,004194: 
025311,004195:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
025312,004196:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
025313,004197:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
025314,004198:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
025315,004199:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
025316,004200: 
025317,004201: 
025318,004202:                                                                                                  #  EXIT  - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025319,004203: 
025320,004204: 
025321,004205:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025322,004206: 
025323,004207:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025324,004208:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025325,004209:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025326,004210: 
025327,004211:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025328,004212:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025329,004213:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025330,004214:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025331,004215: 
025332,004216:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
025333,004217:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
025334,004218:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
025335,004219:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
025336,004220:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
025337,004221: 
025338,004222: 
025339,004223: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025340,004224: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025341,004225: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025342,004226: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025343,004227: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025344,004228:

Page 592

025557,004441:    6030           03041 66107  VB56CADR           2CADR    TRMTRACK

025560,004444:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29  (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025561,004445:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2       BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025562,004446: 
025563,004447: 
025564,004448:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025565,004449: 
025566,004450:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025567,004451:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025568,004452:                                                                                                  #  THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025569,004453:                                                                                                  #  THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025570,004454:                                                                                                  #  DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025571,004455:                                                                                                  #  INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025572,004456: 
025573,004457:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025574,004458: 
025575,004459: 
025576,004460:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025577,004461: 
025578,004462:                                                                                                  #  REMODE   RRTONLY
025579,004463:                                                                                                  #  UNIT     MPACVBUF
025580,004464:                                                                                                  #  QUICTRIG AX*SR*T
025581,004465:                                                                                                  #  SPSIN    SPCOS
025582,004466:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR RROUT
025583,004467:                                                                                                  #  RRRDOT   RRRANGE
025584,004468: 
025585,004469: 
025586,004470:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025587,004471: 
025588,004472: 
025589,004473:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025590,004474: 
025591,004475:                                                                                                  #  RM       RDOTM                  (RAW)
025592,004476:                                                                                                  #  AIG      AMG
025593,004477:                                                                                                  #  AOG      TRKMKCNT               TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025594,004478:                                                                                                  #  TANGNB   TANGNB +1              OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025595,004479:                                                                                                  #  MKTIME
025596,004480:

Page 598 

025598,004482: 
025599,004483:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025600,004484: 
025601,004485:                                                                                                  #  NOR29FLG READRFLG               (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START)  (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025602,004486:                                                                                                  #  PIPTIME  RADMODES (BIT 10)      (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025603,004487:                                                                                                  #  R(CSM)   V(CSM)
025604,004488:                                                                                                  #  R        V                      (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025605,004489: 
025606,004490: 
025607,004491:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025608,004492: 
025609,004493:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 10)
025610,004494:                                                                                                  #  LOSSM    LOSVDT/4       (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025611,004495:                                                                                                  #  SAVECDUT OLDESFLG       (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025612,004496:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG READRFLG
025613,004497: 
025614,004498: 
025615,004499:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025616,004500: 
025617,004501: 
025618,004502:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025619,004503:

025622,004506:                                                                                                  #  RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.

025802,004686:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025803,004687: 
025804,004688:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025805,004689:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025806,004690:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025807,004691:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025808,004692:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025809,004693: 
025810,004694:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025811,004695:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025812,004696: 
025813,004697: 
025814,004698: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025815,004699: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025816,004700: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025817,004701: 
025818,004702: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025819,004703: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025820,004704: 
025821,004705: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025822,004706: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025823,004707: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025824,004708: 
025825,004709: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025826,004710: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025827,004711: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025828,004712: 32,2556           12564                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025829,004713: 
025830,004714: 32,2557           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025831,004715: 32,2560           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025832,004716: 32,2561           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025833,004717: 32,2562           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025834,004718: 32,2563           21101                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025835,004719: 
025836,004720: 32,2564           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025837,004721: 32,2565           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025838,004722: 32,2566           31101                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025839,004723: 32,2567           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025840,004724: 32,2570           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025841,004725: 32,2571           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025842,004726: 32,2572           12600                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025843,004727: 
025844,004728: 32,2573           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025845,004729: 32,2574           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025846,004730: 32,2575           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025847,004731: 32,2576           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025848,004732: 32,2577           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025849,004733: 
025850,004734: 32,2600           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025851,004735: 32,2601           12553                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025852,004736:

Page 604 

025854,004738:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025855,004739: 
025856,004740: 32,2602           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         
025857,004741: 32,2603           52155                           DXCH     MPAC                                  
025858,004742: 32,2604           32775                           CA       R29FXLOC                              #  = ADRES INTB15 + -34D
025859,004743: 32,2605           54120                           TS       FIXLOC                                
025860,004744: 32,2606           04713                           TC       USPRCADR                              #  WITH FIXLOC ARMED FOR LENGTH AND LENGTH
025861,004745: 32,2607           01023                           CADR     UNIT                                  #  SQUARED, BORROW UNITIZING ROUTINE.
025862,004746: 32,2610           07535                           TC       MPACVBUF                              #  MOVE UNIT(LOS) TO AX*SR*T ARG AREA.
025863,004747: 
025864,004748: 32,2611           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025865,004749: 32,2612           12614                           TCF      +2                                    
025866,004750: 32,2613           12630                           TCF      GOTANGLS                              #  GET CDU ANGLES ONLY AFTER 1ST PASS.
025867,004751: 32,2614           00004                           INHINT                                         #  ENSURE CONSISTENT CDU READINGS.
